	//Summary: Returns the absolute URL to use for prefixing any Ajax URL call.
	//Description: Dojo does not handle the case where the parameters in the URL are delimeted by the "/" forward slash. Therefore, in order to
	//             workaround the issue, all AJAX requests must be done using absolute URLs rather than relative.
	//Returns: The absolute URL to use for prefixing any Ajax URL call.
	function getAbsoluteURL() {
		if (absoluteURL != "") {
			var currentURL = document.URL;
			var currentProtocol = "";
		
			if (currentURL.indexOf("://") != -1) {
				currentProtocol = currentURL.substring(0, currentURL.indexOf("://"));
			}
			
			var savedProtocol = "";
			if (absoluteURL.indexOf("://") != -1) {
				savedProtocol = absoluteURL.substring(0, absoluteURL.indexOf("://"));
			}
			
			if (currentProtocol != savedProtocol) {
				absoluteURL = currentProtocol + absoluteURL.substring(absoluteURL.indexOf("://"));
			}
		}
		
		return absoluteURL;
	}
	//Summary: Returns the path pointing to the shared image directory.

	//Returns: The path to reference color-dependant image files.
	function getStyleDirectoryPath() {
		return styleDirectoryPath;
	}

<script type="text/javascript">
	require(["dojo/domReady!"], function(ready){
		dojo.ready(function(){
			var divList = $("#fullCart_accnt_menu li");
			if(divList != null && divList != undefined){
				divList.sort(function(x, y){ 
					var xVar=$(x).find('a').html().toUpperCase();
					var yVar=$(y).find('a').html().toUpperCase();					
				    if(xVar == yVar) return 0;
				    return xVar > yVar? 1: -1;
				});
				$("#fullCart_accnt_menu").html(divList);
			}		
		});		
	});
$(function(){	
function breakAccountOverflow(elem) {
	var tooltip = elem.next(),
		top = elem.offset().top + 30 ,
		left = elem.offset().left - 10;
	tooltip.clone().appendTo($('body'));
	//console.log(tooltip);
	$('body > .termsAccountDetailTooltip').css({
		position: 'absolute',
		left: left+'px',
		top: top+'px',
		bottom: 'auto',
		right: 'auto',
		'z-index': 101,
		'opacity': 1,
		'visibility': 'visible' 
	});
}
$(document).on("mouseover", ".termsAccountDetail", function(e){
	 if(this.offsetWidth < this.scrollWidth){
	  	$('body > .termsAccountDetailTooltip').remove();
		var elem = $(this);
		breakAccountOverflow(elem);
	}
});

$(document).on("mouseout", ".termsAccountDetail", function(e){
	$('body > .termsAccountDetailTooltip').remove();
}); 
		
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	require(["dojo/domReady!"], function(ready){
		dojo.ready(function(){
			var divList = $("#fullCart_accnt_menu li");
			if(divList != null && divList != undefined){
				divList.sort(function(x, y){ 
					var xVar=$(x).find('a').html().toUpperCase();
					var yVar=$(y).find('a').html().toUpperCase();					
				    if(xVar == yVar) return 0;
				    return xVar > yVar? 1: -1;
				});
				$("#fullCart_accnt_menu").html(divList);
			}		
		});		
	});
$(function(){	
function breakAccountOverflow(elem) {
	var tooltip = elem.next(),
		top = elem.offset().top + 30 ,
		left = elem.offset().left - 10;
	tooltip.clone().appendTo($('body'));
	//console.log(tooltip);
	$('body > .termsAccountDetailTooltip').css({
		position: 'absolute',
		left: left+'px',
		top: top+'px',
		bottom: 'auto',
		right: 'auto',
		'z-index': 101,
		'opacity': 1,
		'visibility': 'visible' 
	});
}
$(document).on("mouseover", ".termsAccountDetail", function(e){
	 if(this.offsetWidth < this.scrollWidth){
	  	$('body > .termsAccountDetailTooltip').remove();
		var elem = $(this);
		breakAccountOverflow(elem);
	}
});

$(document).on("mouseout", ".termsAccountDetail", function(e){
	$('body > .termsAccountDetailTooltip').remove();
});

function closePopUp(catentryId){
document.getElementById('avn_stkpopUp_'+catentryId).className="StkPopup hide";
document.getElementById('TTconnect_'+catentryId).className="stkToolTipCon hide";
document.getElementById('check_'+catentryId).value= "N";
}

});
